### 3-206: Beach and Plinth

* A black sand beach stretches along the north bank of this utterly dark cavern.
	* Up the beach is a 5’-square plinth for a statue; all that remains is a 3’ section representing the feet and lower legs of a bipedal figure and an iron rod, rising another 7’ from the center of the plinth.
		* Other pieces of the statue could be remounted on the rod.
			* Top (3-223); second portion (3-205); bottom portion (3-221), eyes (hag’s lair, 3-204).
	* Digging in the sand will produce something interesting once every 3-12 turns (max 3 finds).  Roll on the table.
* 50% chance that Androsia, the greenhag (3-204), is present on the beach.
	* If their mistress is present, the scrags (3-205) lurk near the beach, ready to aid her.
	* If encountered on the beach, she tries to pretend to be a frail, crazy but harmless old hermit, and asks visitors to help her retrieve her staff from the pool.
		* If they comply, the scrags rise to the attack and she shows her true colors.

Statue of Nertet-Indra
* If the pieces are reassembled, they will form a statue of Nertet-Indra, high priestess of Thoth, standing 10' tall, with arms folded across her chest holding ankhs and a tall cylindrical hat.
	* Only once her eyes are restored will the magic in the statue become manifest.
	* In essence, she is a head of Thoth (new) mounted on a full statue.
* As a Head of Thoth, Nertet-Indra retains her personality.
	* She eagerly questions, and answers questions about the history of the cult of Thoth.
		* Who reigns in the halls (especially Levels 2 and 3), what has become of the priests, what god the PCs worship, what their intentions are, and what they might do to restore the cult of Thoth.
	* She attributes the slow demise of the city to the insidious influence of Set, and offers advice on how to stamp out Set and his followers.
		* Only too aware of the power of Set during her own day, she is able to give clear information about the Set temple and neighboring precincts.
	* She can provide a good general layout of Levels 1-3.
	* If treated well, Nertet-Indra will be willing to incant a Blessing of Thoth three times per day; healing 3-18 damage and curing all poisons.

D10 Find
1 1-3 black pearls, worth 100-1,000 gp each
2 a piece of jewelry worth 50-300 gp
3 a leather pouch with 255 gp worth mixed coins
4 a gold holy symbol of either Set or Thoth (50 gp)
5 a rusted ordinary weapon
6 an ivory scroll case (35 gp), 50% chance to contain a scroll of 2-5 spells
7 a random piece of equipment, 25% chance spoiled
8 a minor magic item (GM’s choice)
9 a magical potion (GM’s choice)
10 a magical weapon (GM’s choice)

### 3-207: Misty Cave

* This large cave is filled with a thick white mist, evident from every entryway.
	* Those breathing the mist must saving vs poison or be confused for 1d6 turns (roll d10 on chart).
		* 1-2 Attack nearest
		* 3-4 Sit in catatonic state
		* 5-8 Walk at full movement for duration, rolling for direction each turn
		* 9-10 Walk at full movement, discarding one piece of equipment per turn

### 3-208: Mud Pool

* This low-lying cavern contains a 10’-wide by 18’-long pool of light-brown mud.
	* The mud radiates heat, and detects as magic.
	* If disturbed, three mud people (new) rise and attack (1 per round for three rounds).
		* They will pursue enemies within the river caves.
	* At the bottom of the pool is a silver necklace decorated with dangling azurite (450 gp), and a bone scroll casing (scroll of protection from magic).

3 mud people (see new monsters): SZ M; AL N; AC 4; MV 90’; HD 3; HP 22, 18, 15; #AT 2; Dmg 1-8/1-8. Special attacks: hurl mud blobs; drown foes in mud. Special defenses: regenerate 2 HP/rd while touching mud; half damage from edged weapons, and from fire and electricity.

### 3-209: Pillared Caves

* Both lobes of this cavern contain an onyx column atop a stone pedestal, each pedestal with an obvious front, on which is carved a question mark.
	* The columns are composed of five 2’-thick sections mounted on top of each other on an iron rod stuck into the pedestalm each with fives faces that can be rotated independently.  Each section's faces show a distinct carving: a winged horse (pegasus), a ram, an iguana, a snake and a cat.
* The correct combination is to turn the faces, from top to bottom, toward the question mark in the order Pegasus-Ram-Iguana-Snake-Cat (i.e. PRISC, short for Priscus).
	* If done on one column, a voice rumbles (Mithric) “Priscus Pulcher offers his friends the gift of Perception”, and detect illusion is cast on all within 10’ (2d6 hours).
	* If done on both columns, in addition the columns will bestow a +2 to the next 5 rolls of each person within 10 feet.
	* These effects can only be produced once per week.
	* GM Note: the purpose of this puzzle was to provide the enlightened assistance in penetrating the illusionary wall in 3-196.

### 3-210: Lichen Cave

* This large cave is relatively flat, with no stalactites or stalagmites.
	* It is infested with a colony of benign light-green lichen that gives off a soft glow.
		* Edible and nutritious, but not very appetizing.

## Level 3: 211 - 231

### 3-211: Crossroads

* This set of tunnels is damp and warm.
	* The passage to the west has collapsed.
	* The passage to the east is quite narrow at its opening (only 2’ wide).
	* The passage to the south becomes a worked corridor after a short distance, before ending in a locked door to 3-195.

### 3-212: Half-Finished Cave

* This area contains another section of never-completed Thothian construction.
	* The room has been squared and smoothed, and four 3’-deep and 2’-diameter holes have been excavated.  The purpose of the holes, and the room, is unclear.
	* Signs of traffic are evident leading between the west and south doors.
	* Both doors are locked, and well oiled.

##### 3-212a: Stairs Down to 4-159 

* This narrow stair leads downward to 4-159. 

### 3-213: Black Light Zombies

* This cavern slopes downward to the west and is noticeably colder than the surrounding chambers.
	* A 3’-tall rock-crystal lamp (a black light of useful necromancy, new) stands in the middle of the room, emitting strange black light.
		* In this light, undead regenerate 2 hp/round.
		* The lamp has 5 hp and ceases to shine if broken.
	* An ancient Thothian labor force of 12 zombies that was excavating 3-212 stands idle.
		* They attack anyone not wearing the ceremonial robes of Thoth, but will not leave the chamber.
		* They are armed with picks, hammers, and similar implements.

12 zombies: SZ M; AL N; AC 8; MV 60’; HD 2; HP 14, 14 12(x3), 11(x3), 10, 10, 9, 9; #AT 1; Dmg 1-8. Special: always strike last; regenerate while in the black light.

### 3-214: Rope Trick

* A rope dangles from mid-air in the middle of this non-descript cave.
	* It is a rope trick rope. Pulling the rope pulls three adventurers from the extra-dimensional space, surprised and ill-disposed (-15% reaction).

GM Note: Roscoe and his friends fell into trouble in the Forum of Set when they inadvertently insulted the Master of the Guild of Service and couldn’t pay the necessary fine.
* Although they lost two members of the party, the remainder got lucky and managed to flee down the Long Stair (4-19) to 4-163, then east to 4-159 and finally to this cave.
* They have good knowledge about Level 4, particularly the direct route from 4-190 through 4-120 and on to the Forum, and, of course, their escape route.
* Their former comrade, Azgallatu, was taken by the setites and is imprisoned in 3-105.

Roscoe, 3rd-level male Thorcin fighter: SZ M; AL LN; AC 5; MV 60’; HD 3; HP 27; #AT 1; Dmg 1-6 (short bow and arrows), 2-7 (short sword, short bow and +1 arrows). Abilities: STR 17, INT 9, WIS 12, DEX 10, CON 16, CHA 11. 
* Possessions: scale mail and shield; spear; short sword; short bow with 15 normal arrows and 5 +1 arrows; a purse with 35 sp and 120 gp; and a troll thegn’s passport (see Arden Vul items).

Trillip, 3rd-level female Wiskin magic user: SZ M; AL LN; AC 7; MV 120’; HD 3; HP 9; #AT 1; Dmg 1-6 (staff), 1-3 (darts). Abilities: STR 10, INT 16, WIS 9, DEX 16, CON 14, CHA 11. 
* Possessions: staff; 10 darts; ring of protection +1; potion of flying; a purse with three 100 gp pearls, 25 sp, and 150 gp. Spells memorized: magic missile, sleep; rope trick. Spell book: comprehend languages, detect magic, erase, magic missile, magic aura, read magic, shield, sleep; continual light, knock, rope trick; slow.

Iris, 5th-level female Thorcin thief: SZ M; AL NE; AC 4; MV 120’; HD 3; HP 15; #AT 1; Dmg 2-9 (long sword), 3-6 (sling); Abilities: STR 16, INT 9, WIS 13, DEX 18, CON 15, CHA 6. 
* Thief skills: PP 60%, OL 57%, F/RT 45%, MS 50%, HS 41%, HN 20%, CW 90%, RL 25%. 
* Possessions: leather armor; long sword; sling with 20 bullets; a potion of climbing; a purse with 35 sp, 15 ancient silver pennies (see Arden Vul items), 75 gp, 5 octagonal platinum coins, a platinum key to the Obsidian Gates (5-6D), and a copper rudishva identity plaque (see new technological items).

### 3-215: Skeletal Corpses

* This partly finished cave has a rough stone floor, walls, and a crude stone door on the south wall.
	* In the center a solid-gold, 3' tall statuette sits on a greasy crocodile-hide mat.
		* The icon depicts a cat sitting on its hind legs, solid gold with small jet gems for eyes and nose
		* It is a statuette of Bastet (new).
			* Touching (non-Mi'it) it causes a spirit cat to rake you for 2d4 and save vs poison at +2 or die, 3d8 on success.
			* Being near one begins hearing telepathic cat noises; listen long enough and they speak “Avenge this wrong. Return me to my sister-people. Touching me is forbidden!.”  Returning it to the shrine of Bastet (8-38) brings a reward.
	* Around the statuette, and partly on the mat, are four badly decomposed corpses - 3 adventurers and a cave skink.
		* The adventurers have no equipment, as the hag and her minions stole all of it. 
		* The corpses are mostly decomposed, but close examination of the face of one reveals it was raked, as if by sharp claws.
			* The human corpses are of adventurers who stole the statuette and brought it here to examine.  When they touched their prize it inflicted serious - and poisonous - scratches on their faces and bodies.
		* The cave skink had the misfortune to brush against the statuette.

### 3-216: Penned Pudding

* The entrance to this lobed cavern is blocked by a buzzing force field of magical energy.
	* Ancient Thothian mages erected the wall of force to pen a particularly large black pudding for future use and/or study.
		* It is beginning to fray, and collapses if struck hard (such as an open doors check, or a mace blow).
	* If the field is removed, the pudding flows swiftly along the ceiling to drop down on an advancing party.
	* The cavern is unremarkable, except being noticeably free of dust and dirt.

1 black pudding: SZ M; AL N; AC 6; MV 60’; HD 10; HP 50; #AT 1; Dmg 3-24. Special attacks: dissolve wood and metal. Special defenses: divide into parts when struck; immune to cold.

X / 50
### 3-217: The Seamly Run

* In this section, the Seamly Run wends its way through a narrow (5’-wide) but deep (10’-deep) channel.
	* The current is swift.  Those who fall in are borne quickly to the beach at 3-206, taking 1d6 HP from buffeting along the way.

### 3-218: River Cave

* This damp and humid cave holds a shallow puddle along the south wall, occasionally refreshed by seepage from the Seamly Run.
	* Twenty voracious cave skinks live here (only 5-10 present at any given time).
	* They are able to run along walls and like to ‘fish’ in the Seamly Run.
	* They fear the scrags (3-206) and likely flee to the river if noise emerges from the direction of 3-219 or 3-220.  Within 5 rounds, hunger conquers fear, and they return in search of nourishment.

5-10 cave skinks (see new monsters): SZ S; AL N; AC 7; MV 120’; HD 2; HP 15, 14, 13, 13, 12(x3), 11, 11, 10; #AT 1; Dmg 1-6. Special attacks: toxic mucus.

### 3-219: Warning Sign

* This river cave marks the western edge of the territory of Androsia, the Hag.
	* A femur thrust into a hole in the uneven floor marks the boundary; on top of the femur is a beastman skull.
	* A variety of small animal bones (salamanders, mostly) litters the cave. 

### 3-220: Unfinished Hall

* The priests of Thoth began to work this chamber, but abandoned it before completion.
	* Sections of smooth, rectilinear wall adjoin rough, natural cavern walls.
	* A pair of wooden wheelbarrows stands in the mouth of the east-leading corridor; they contain some dusty mining tools (hammers, picks, pitons, etc.).
	* The rest of the hall is dusty, with clear footprints in the dust (scrag prints) leading towards 3-219.
	* The remains of two adventurers (killed by scrags) lie against the southwestern wall.
		* Short sword +2, a sapphire Sortian eye; a purse (57 sp, 43 gp)
		* A parchment with (Archontean) “red-black-yellow-blue-green-white” (the ‘address’ to the teleportation ring at SL6-28)
		* A map of the eastern precincts of Thoth (3-43 to 3-51, including 3-50, 3-50a and 3-50b).

##### 3-220a: Blocked Corridor

* The corridor to the east is blocked with rubble.
	* An old, brittle skeleton clad in orange Thothian robes lies on the floor of the unfinished corridor that leads to the north.

### 3-221: Gaunt Beastmen

* A moist and dank cave, covered with a strange blue mold.
	* A patrol of beastmen from the Long Range Cavern Patrol (3-154) dwells here, charmed by the greenhag (3-204).
		* They have lost their discipline and are slowly starving to death, subsisting barely on the blue mold.
		* Only Histar, their sergeant, retains a dim sense of his former life and purpose.
		* They have a campfire, but little fuel for it.
		* 15% chance the beastmen are out at 3-222.
		* If the hag is killed, 75% likely the beastmen have fled back to the Tagma.
		* Trisko the Natty of the LRCP is eager for news of his missing patrol.
	* The upper thighs / lower torso portion of the statue of Nertet-Indra (3-206) is discarded in the corner.

7 enslaved beastman troopers (see new monsters): SZ S; AL LN; AC 6; MV 90’; HD 1+1; HP: 6, 5, 5, 4, 4, 3, 3; #AT 1; Dmg 1-6. Special attacks: tactics. Possessions: ring mail and shield; 
spears; short swords; short bows.

Histar, enslaved beastman sergeant (see new monsters): SZ S; AL LN; AC 4; MV 90’: HD 2+2; HP 15; #AT 1; Dmg 1-6 or 2-5. Special attacks: tactics. Possessions: ring mail and shield; spear; war hammer.

### 3-222: Cave of Bones

* This large cave has a 15’ ceiling and is covered with a 2’-deep carpet of bones.
	* The bones are of varied size and origin; some quite ancient, others fresh.
	* Androsia the hag (3-204) and her entourage have deposited centuries worth of bodies in this cave.
	* Movement is slow and noisy. A quasi-palpable aura of dread and/or evil may be felt.
	* Hard to notice, hanging from a rock projection on the north wall is a ruby pendant (1750 gp).
		* Actually a hag’s eye (new) allowing Androsia to see events in the cave of bones. 
			* Can see and locate when w/in half a mile.
			* A mage can take possession of it for 1000 gp and 1d6 permanent hp.
			* Breaking it deals its owner 2d6 and blindness for 2d6 days.
* 15% chance Androsia the greenhag is present, gnawing on some bones.
	* If so, the ogres (3-223) and beastmen (3-221) are present with her.

### 3-223: Emaciated Ogres

* A small group of ogres, charmed by Androsia the greenhag (3-204), inhabits this extended cavern.
	* Explorers may (2 in 6) notice the odor of smoked meat 10’ into the cave; the odor is automatically noticeable after 30’.
	* The ogres have rigged a deadfall trap (marked X) in the first portion of their cave
		* A skeleton wearing a fine pair of maroon leather boots (25 gp) lies beneath the deadfall as bait.
		* Slighly disturbing it trigger 50% of the time, more serious manipulating 80%.
		* Rocks fall for 2d6 and save vs transform or pinned.
		* At the clatter, the ogres rush ravenously from the eastern cave.
	* The ogres’ actual lair lies east, where a feeble fire burns in a pile of bones.
		* They are curing a human corpse, suspended from a hook directly over the fire. 
		* They have a sack in which they keep their pitiful treasure.
			* 451 cp, four 100 gp aquamarines, 2 pieces of valueless colored glass, and an iron necklace (10 cp).
		* Lying among the carnage is the stone head of the statue of Nertet-Indra (3-206).
			* The head is of a human female wearing a tall cylindrical hat. Her eyes are almond, but hollow.
* 15% chance the ogres are present w/ Androsia in 3-222.
	* If the hag is killed, the ogres will likely (70%) have fled, taking with them their sack (but leaving the stone head and the leather boots).

6 emaciated ogres: SZ L; AL CE; AC 5; MV 90’; HD 4+1; HP 27, 25, 22, 19, 18, 15; #AT 1; Dmg 1-10, or by weapon.
* Actually alchemically overgrown goblins.

### 3-224: Antechamber to the Hag’s Domain

* This cave is noticeably cooler than the caves to the east.
	* A quasi-palpable aura of evil may be detected here, just as in 3-222.
	* A 6’ iron rod has been thrust into the middle of the cave floor; the body of an ogre impaled upon it (despite decomposition, it was clearly badly malnourished).
		* Androsia the hag (3-204) placed it here as a warning to both to her slaves and to intruders.

### 3-225: Dead Cube 

* A dead gelatinous cube is slowly deliquescing on the floor of this flat cave. A pack of giant rats is feasting on the tasty remains.
	* In its mass: 63 cp, a single bracer from a pair of bracers of haste (new).
		* The bracer is inoperable without its companion, worn by Killik the goblin (5-46).

15 giant rats: SZ S; AL N(E); AC 7; MV 120’; HD 1-4 HP; HP 4(x4), 3(x4), 2(x4), 1(x3); #At 1; Dmg 1-3. Special attacks: 5% chance of disease.

### 3-226: Empty Cave

* This cave contains numerous stalagmites.
	* If searched, a partially-encased gold ring (50 gp) can be extracted from one of the stalagmite after 1-3 turns of chipping at the rock.

### 3-227: Lizard Nest

* This cave is connected to the Great Cavern (3-163) by a fairly wide but short tunnel.
	* The entrance to the tunnel is partly concealed by giant mushrooms.
	* A group of 5 subterranean lizards make their lair in this small cave, in a nest built of sticks, dung, and dirt.
		* Only one lizard is present at any one time.
			* Noisy combat here will draw two more from 3-229 in 3 rounds.
		* In the lizard nest: 2 subterranean lizard eggs, plus a solid gold egg (200 gp).

1-3 subterranean lizards: SZ L; AL N; AC 5; MV 120’; HD 6; HP 45, 40, 39; #AT 1; Dmg 2-12. Special attacks: double damage on a natural roll to hit of 20.

### 3-228: Wounded Fungal Foresters

* Four wounded fungal foresters (new), defeated by the subterranean lizards in 3-229, have retreated to this chamber to rest and recuperate.

3 wounded spotted fungal foresters (see new monsters): SZ S; AL N; AC 6; MV 30’ on rock, 90’ in fungal forests; HD 4; HP 14, 13, 9; #AT 1; Dmg 2-12.

1 wounded blue fungal forester (see new monsters): SZ M; AL N; AC 6; MV 30’ on rock, 90’ in fungal forests; HD 6; HP 19; #AT 1; Dmg 2-12. Special attacks: spore cloud (stun).

### 3-229: Feeding Frenzy

* Two subterranean lizards are feeding on the bodies of two fungal foresters in this non-descript cave.
	* If encountered first in 3-227, the lizards are not present here.

2 subterranean lizards: SZ L; AL N; AC 5; MV 120’; HD 6; HP 37, 35; #AT 1; Dmg 2-12. Special attacks: double damage on a natural roll to hit of 20.

X / 37
X / 35
X / 39
### 3-230: The Seamly Run 

* The Seamly Run is a swift-flowing river that runs through this level.
	* It is filled with cold, clear water.
	* The current between 3-205 and 3-164 is quite strong.

### 3-231: Swift Current and River Exit

* Here the river exits the great cavern through a 7’-diameter tunnel.
	* The current entering the tunnel is quite strong; swimmers anywhere near the tunnel mouth roll 3d8 under DEX or STR to avoid being swept into the tunnel.
		* The river’s exit from level 3 is a relatively narrow crack in the granite; persons stuck in the tunnel will drown in 1d3 rounds unless rescued.
		* A staff of the frog (new) is wedged in the crack.
	* The Seamly Run is impassable after this point, entering a series of small, vertical shafts before eventually joining a vast dark sea in the Underearth.
